NOTIFICATION BY THE ELECTION COMMISSION OF INDIA
ELECTION SYMBOLS (RESERVATION & ALLOTMENT) ORDER, 1968
No. SRO G-31/2025.
The following Notification of the Election Commission of India, Nirvachan Sadan, Ashoka Road, New Delhi - 110 001, 
dated 10th October, 2025 [18 Asvina, 1947 (Saka)] is republished:-
No.56/2025/PPS-III :-  WHEREAS, the Election Commission of India has decided to update its Notification 
No.56/2024/PPS-III, dated 27th March, 2024, specifying the names of registered un-recognized parties [RUPPs], issued 
in pursuance of paragraph 17 of the Election Symbols (Reservation and Allotment) Order, 1968;
 NOW, THEREFORE, in pursuance of paragraph 17 of the Election Symbols (Reservation and Allotment) Order, 
1968, and in supersession of its aforesaid notification No.56/2024/PPS-III, dated 27th March, 2024, published in the 
Gazette of India, Extra-Ordinary, Part-II, Section-3, Sub-Section (iii), the Election Commission of India hereby specifies: -
(a)	 In Table I (A), the registered un-recognized political parties [RUPPs] and postal address of their 
Headquarters; 
(b)	 In Table I (B), the list of 334 delisted registered unrecognized political parties [RUPPs] and postal address 
of their Headquarters; and
(c)	 In Table I (C), the list of 474 delisted registered unrecognized political parties [RUPPs] and postal address 
of their Headquarters;.
(By Order)
	
Soumyajit Ghosh,
	
Secretary, 
	
Election Commission of India.
Secretariat,	
	
ARCHANA PATNAIK, 
Chennai-600 009, 
Chief Electoral Officer and
14th October, 2025.	
Secretary to Government, 
	
	
	
Public (Elections) Department.

As per the Commission’s Order dated 09.08.2025, the registered unrecognized political parties mentioned 
therein have been removed from the list after following due process:
All Chief Electoral Officers and Returning Officers are advised that if any registered unrecognized political party, 
which has been removed from the said list, approaches for the allotment of a Common Symbol, the matter shall be 
dealt with in accordance with the Commission’s Order dated 09.08.2025, with due diligence and proper procedure.
For the registered unrecognized political parties that have been removed from the list, the prescribed Forms ‘A’ 
and ‘B’ for claiming a Common Symbol have become inoperative.

TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY
125
According to the Commission’s Order dated 19.09.2025, the registered unrecognized political parties 
mentioned therein have been removed from the list after following due process: 
All Chief Electoral Officers and Returning Officers are advised that if any political party removed from the said list 
approaches for the allotment of a Common Symbol, the matter should be dealt with in accordance with the Commission’s 
Order dated 19.09.2025, with due diligence and proper procedure.
For the registered unrecognized political parties that have been removed from the list, the prescribed 
Forms ‘A’ and ‘B’ for claiming a Common Symbol have become inoperative.
(By Order)
	
Soumyajit Ghosh, 
	
Secretary, 
	
Election Commission of India.
Secretariat, 	
	
ARCHANA PATNAIK, 
Chennai-600 009,  
Chief Electoral Officer and
14th October, 2025.	
Secretary to Government, 
	
	
	
Public (Elections) Department.
